cat > /tmp/test_dst.mjs << 'EOF'
import * as dateFns from 'date-fns';

// Simulate the old behavior (addHours)
function oldMeridiemConversion(dateToTransferFrom, dateToTransferTo) {
    const isAM = dateFns.getHours(dateToTransferFrom) < 12;
    const mergedDateHours = dateFns.getHours(dateToTransferTo);

    if (isAM && mergedDateHours >= 12) {
        return dateFns.addHours(dateToTransferTo, -12);
    }

    if (!isAM && mergedDateHours < 12) {
        return dateFns.addHours(dateToTransferTo, 12);
    }

    return dateToTransferTo;
}

// Simulate the new behavior (setHours)
function newMeridiemConversion(dateToTransferFrom, dateToTransferTo) {
    const isAM = dateFns.getHours(dateToTransferFrom) < 12;
    const mergedDateHours = dateFns.getHours(dateToTransferTo);

    if (isAM && mergedDateHours >= 12) {
        return dateFns.setHours(dateToTransferTo, mergedDateHours - 12);
    }

    if (!isAM && mergedDateHours < 12) {
        return dateFns.setHours(dateToTransferTo, mergedDateHours + 12);
    }

    return dateToTransferTo;
}

// Test: March 8, 2026 12:00 PM (DST day), change to AM
console.log('=== Test 1: 12 PM -> AM on DST day ===');
const dateFrom = new Date(2026, 2, 8, 0, 0, 0); // '12 AM' parsed representation
const dateTo = new Date(2026, 2, 8, 12, 0, 0); // 12 PM reference date

const oldResult = oldMeridiemConversion(dateFrom, dateTo);
console.log('Old result:', dateFns.getHours(oldResult), 'hours, local:', oldResult.toLocaleString());

const newResult = newMeridiemConversion(dateFrom, dateTo);
console.log('New result:', dateFns.getHours(newResult), 'hours, local:', newResult.toLocaleString());

// Test: 12 AM -> PM on DST day
console.log('\n=== Test 2: 12 AM -> PM on DST day ===');
const dateFrom2 = new Date(2026, 2, 8, 12, 0, 0); // '12 PM' parsed
const dateTo2 = new Date(2026, 2, 8, 0, 0, 0); // 12 AM reference

const oldResult2 = oldMeridiemConversion(dateFrom2, dateTo2);
console.log('Old result:', dateFns.getHours(oldResult2), 'hours, local:', oldResult2.toLocaleString());

const newResult2 = newMeridiemConversion(dateFrom2, dateTo2);
console.log('New result:', dateFns.getHours(newResult2), 'hours, local:', newResult2.toLocaleString());

// Test: Normal day (not DST)
console.log('\n=== Test 3: 12 PM -> AM on non-DST day ===');

cd /testbed/packages/x-date-pickers && TZ=America/New_York node -e '
const dateFns = require("date-fns");

// Simulate the old behavior (addHours)
function oldMeridiemConversion(dateToTransferFrom, dateToTransferTo) {
    const isAM = dateFns.getHours(dateToTransferFrom) < 12;
    const mergedDateHours = dateFns.getHours(dateToTransferTo);

    if (isAM && mergedDateHours >= 12) {
        return dateFns.addHours(dateToTransferTo, -12);
    }

    if (!isAM && mergedDateHours < 12) {
        return dateFns.addHours(dateToTransferTo, 12);
    }

    return dateToTransferTo;
}

// Simulate the new behavior (setHours)
function newMeridiemConversion(dateToTransferFrom, dateToTransferTo) {
    const isAM = dateFns.getHours(dateToTransferFrom) < 12;
    const mergedDateHours = dateFns.getHours(dateToTransferTo);

    if (isAM && mergedDateHours >= 12) {
        return dateFns.setHours(dateToTransferTo, mergedDateHours - 12);
    }

    if (!isAM && mergedDateHours < 12) {
        return dateFns.setHours(dateToTransferTo, mergedDateHours + 12);
    }

    return dateToTransferTo;
}

// Test: March 8, 2026 12:00 PM (DST day), change to AM
console.log("=== Test 1: 12 PM -> AM on DST day ===");
const dateFrom = new Date(2026, 2, 8, 0, 0, 0);
const dateTo = new Date(2026, 2, 8, 12, 0, 0);

const oldResult = oldMeridiemConversion(dateFrom, dateTo);
console.log("Old result:", dateFns.getHours(oldResult), "hours, local:", oldResult.toLocaleString());

const newResult = newMeridiemConversion(dateFrom, dateTo);
console.log("New result:", dateFns.getHours(newResult), "hours, local:", newResult.toLocaleString());

// Test: 12 AM -> PM on DST day
console.log("\n=== Test 2: 12 AM -> PM on DST day ===");
const dateFrom2 = new Date(2026, 2, 8, 12, 0, 0);
const dateTo2 = new Date(2026, 2, 8, 0, 0, 0);

const oldResult2 = oldMeridiemConversion(dateFrom2, dateTo2);
console.log("Old result:", dateFns.getHours(oldResult2), "hours, local:", oldResult2.toLocaleString());

const newResult2 = newMeridiemConversion(dateFrom2, dateTo2);
console.log("New result:", dateFns.getHours(newResult2), "hours, local:", newResult2.toLocaleString());

// Test: Normal day

Now, let me double check the `convertToMeridiem` function in `time-utils.ts` to make sure it also handles DST correctly. It uses `setHours` which we've already verified works. But wait, let me look at the `convertValueToMeridiem` helper more carefully:

```typescript
export const convertValueToMeridiem = (value: number, meridiem: Meridiem | null, ampm: boolean) => {
  if (ampm) {
    const currentMeridiem = value >= 12 ? 'pm' : 'am';
    if (currentMeridiem !== meridiem) {
      return meridiem === 'am' ? value - 12 : value + 12;
    }
  }
  return value;
};
```

This correctly converts:
- 12 PM → AM: 12 - 12 = 0 ✓
- 12 AM → PM: 0 + 12 = 12 ✓
- 1 PM → AM: 1 - 12 = -11... Wait, that would be wrong! But that can't happen because if the hour is 1, the current meridiem would be 'am', and we wouldn't try to convert to 'am' again.

Actually, let me check. If we have 1 PM (13:00 in 24h), and we want to convert to AM:
- value = 13 (adapter.getHours returns 13 in 24h format)
- meridiem = 'am'
- currentMeridiem = 'pm' (13 >= 12)
- return 13 - 12 = 1

That gives 1, which is correct (1 AM).

If we have 1 AM (1:00 in 24h), and we want to convert to PM:
- value = 1
- meridiem = 'pm'
- currentMeridiem = 'am' (1 < 12)
- return 1 + 12 = 13

That gives 13, which is correct (1 PM).

All good.

1. **Normal (non-DST) days**: Both old and new code produce the same results (as shown in Test 3).
2. **DST spring forward (March)**: New code correctly uses `setHours` instead of `addHours`.

When switching between AM and PM in a time field, the code used `adapter.addHours(date, ±12)` to adjust the meridiem. However, `addHours` works with absolute time (UTC), not wall-clock time. On days when Daylight Saving Time (DST) transitions occur (like the second Sunday of March when clocks "spring forward"), subtracting 12 hours from noon results in 11 PM the previous day instead of midnight, because the day only has 23 hours.\n\nThe fix replaces `adapter.addHours` with `adapter.setHours`:\n- `adapter.addHours(dateToTransferTo, -12)` → `adapter.setHours(dateToTransferTo, mergedDateHours - 12)`\n- `adapter.addHours(dateToTransferTo, 12)` → `adapter.setHours(dateToTransferTo, mergedDateHours + 12)`\n\n`setHours` sets the wall-clock hour directly, which correctly handles DST transitions because it preserves the date while only changing the hour value.\n\nThis fix was applied to:\n1.
